# Andrews Formula Occurrences

Source PDF: `/Users/jaimenunez/Downloads/Andrews_Introduction_to_Classical_Nahuatl_693p_reOCR_squareZeroFixed.pdf`

Generated: 2026-06-23 from the local 693-page PDF using Python/pypdf to read the OCR text layer, then visually audited against rendered PDF page images for formula material containing zero/square-zero glyphs, uppercase letters, OCR `1`, spaces inside parentheses, non-ellipsis punctuation inside stem material, or formula material split across a line/page break; the line-break reconciliation pass fused wrapped formulas back into one occurrence; the temporary render/extraction cache was not committed.

Scope: this is the exhaustive formula occurrence index for Andrews formula-like material detected in the PDF: hash-bound nuclear-clause formulas, prefixal hash formulas, formula fragments, particle attachment tokens, explicit linear formulas, compound equations, derivational-history schemas, slot-filler fragments, relational templates, translation formulas, external reference formulas, and calendar line formulas. This file is an evidence index, not a polished grammar specification; verify the PDF image before implementing any row. Remaining `hash-fragment` rows are printed fragments or visibly incomplete formulas in Andrews, not unresolved line-wrap continuations.

Authority boundary: Andrews supplies formula architecture only. Do not import Classical spellings from these rows directly into Nawat/Pipil surfaces.

## Visual-Risk Rule

Rows whose formula material contained `0`, OCR `O`, uppercase letters, spaces inside parentheses, OCR `1` inside stem material, non-ellipsis punctuation inside stem material, or formula material split across a line/page break were not accepted from the OCR text layer alone. The visual pass used rendered PDF pages to normalize square-zero glyphs to `[sq0]`, lower-case ell glyphs that OCR read as `I` to `l`, OCR-added spaces inside formula parentheses away from the formula, OCR `1` used for lower-case `l` or `i` in stem material, OCR punctuation where the page image showed letters, hyphens, regular zero, or vowel length, and line/page-broken formula material back into one occurrence. Remaining `hash-fragment` rows are kept only where Andrews itself prints a fragment or visibly omits a closing boundary. Ellipsis placeholders (`...`) are exempt and retained as structural placeholders. Template variables and capitalized proper-name stems are retained when they are visually part of the formula.

Detailed visual-risk row status: `docs/ANDREWS_FORMULA_VISUAL_AUDIT.md`.
